# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Excellent! I've successfully compiled a comprehensive analysis of the Apache Kafka plugin/extension loading system with interface-based dependency injection. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **28 key Java source files** implementing the Kafka plugin architecture in `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka), organized into several categories:

### Core Plugin Interfaces (connect/api)
- **Connector** - Abstract base class for all connector implementations
- **SourceConnector** and **SinkConnector** - Concrete connector types
- **Converter** and **HeaderConverter** - Data serialization plugins
- **Task** - Base interface for task implementations
- **ConnectorContext**, **SourceTaskContext**, **SinkTaskContext** - Dependency injection interfaces

### Plugin Type System
- **PluginType** enum - Defines 9 plugin categories (SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY)
- **PluginDesc<T>** - Generic descriptor holding plugin metadata, class reference, version, and classloader

### Plugin Scanning via Reflection
- **PluginScanner** (abstract) - Base scanning framework with ServiceLoader support
- **ReflectionScanner** - Uses ClassGraph library for reflection-based discovery
- **ServiceLoaderScanner** - Uses Java SPI (META-INF/services) for modern discovery
- **PluginScanResult** - Aggregates discovered plugins by type

### Classloader Hierarchy (Child-First Delegation)
- **PluginClassLoader** - URLClassLoader for isolated plugin loading with child-first delegation
- **DelegatingClassLoader** - Master classloader orchestrating multiple PluginClassLoaders
- **ClassLoaderFactory** - Creates classloader instances with security support
- **PluginSource** - Represents plug
... (truncated)

The `scanPlugins()` method:\\n- Uses ClassGraph to scan all classes in the classloader\\n- Calls `getPluginDesc()` for each plugin type (SINK, SOURCE, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE)\\n- Instantiates plugins to extract version information\\n- Validates classpath consistency\\n\\n**ServiceLoaderScanner** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Implements modern discovery using Java's ServiceLoader mechanism exclusively. The `scanPlugins()` method calls `getServiceLoaderPluginDesc()` for each plugin type, loading plugins declared in `META-INF/services/` manifest files.\\n\\n**PluginScanResult** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Container holding discovered plugins organized by type (SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> for each type).\\n\\n## PluginDesc - Child-First Delegation\\n\\n**PluginClassLoader** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): Custom URLClassLoader implementing child-first classloading:\\n- Loads plugin classes from its own URLs first\\n- Delegates to parent for classes not found or those that shouldn't be isolated\\n- Thread-safe and parallel-capable (marked with `ClassLoader.registerAsParallelCapable()`)\\n- Stores the `pluginLocation` (top-level plugin path) for tracking plugin sources\\n\\n**DelegatingClassLoader** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): Master classloader orchestrating isolation:\\n- Acts as child-first classloader, delegating plugin loading to child PluginClassLoaders\\n- Maintains `pluginLoaders`: ConcurrentMap<String, SortedMap<PluginDesc<?>, ClassLoader>> for managing multiple versions\\n- Maintains `aliases`: ConcurrentMap for plugin name aliases\\n- Methods:\\n  - `installDiscoveredPlugins(scanResult)`: Registers discovered plugins with their classloaders\\n  - `connectorLoader(connectorName)`: Retrieves the classloader for a specific connector\\n\\n**ClassLoaderFactory** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory for creating DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances, with security manager support.\\n\\n## Plugin Source and Isolation Decision\\n\\n**PluginSource** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): Record class representing a plugin source with:\\n- `location`: Path to the plugin directory\\n- `type`: CLASSPATH or ISOLATED\\n- `loader`: ClassLoader for this source\\n- `urls`: Array of URLs to scan\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Utility methods for plugin management:\\n- `shouldLoadInIsolation(className)`: Determines if a class should be loaded in isolation using EXCLUDE/INCLUDE regex patterns\\n- `pluginSources(pluginLocations, delegatingClassLoader, factory)`: Creates PluginSource objects from configured plugin paths\\n- `isolatedPluginSource()` and `classpathPluginSource()`: Factory methods for specific source types\\n- `simpleName()`, `prunedName()`: Plugin naming utilities for aliases\\n\\n## Main Plugin Orchestrator - Creates DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances\\n  - Runs PluginScanner (ReflectionScanner or ServiceLoaderScanner) to discover plugins\\n  - Returns merged PluginScanResult\\n\\n**Plugin Instantiation with Dependency Injection:**\\n- `newPlugin(classOrAlias, range)`: Creates plugin instances with version support\\n  - Resolves plugin aliases\\n  - Uses pluginLoader() to get the appropriate ClassLoader\\n  - Instantiates the plugin class with proper classloader context\\n  - Configurable via LoaderSwap for context switching\\n\\n- `newPlugin(classOrAlias, range, sourceLoader)`: Creates plugins from a specific source classloader\\n\\n- `newConnector()`: Factory for creating Connector instances\\n- `newConverter()`: Factory for creating Converter instances with `configure(config, isKey)` dependency injection\\n- `newHeaderConverter()`: Factory for creating HeaderConverter instances\\n- `newPlugins()`: Batch creation of multiple plugin instances\\n\\n**Plugin Querying:**\\n- `sourceConnectors(alias)`, `sinkConnectors(alias)`: Retrieve connector plugin descriptors\\n- `converters(alias)`, `headerConverters(alias)`: Retrieve converter plugin descriptors\\n- `pluginVersion()`: Get version of a specific plugin\\n- `pluginClass()`: Get the Class<?> of a plugin\\n\\n**Classloader Management:**\\n- `delegatingLoader()`: Returns the master DelegatingClassLoader\\n- `connectorLoader(connectorName)`: Gets the classloader for a connector\\n- `pluginLoader(classOrAlias, range, sourceLoader)`: Internal method resolving the appropriate classloader\\n- `withClassLoader(loader)`: Returns LoaderSwap for temporarily changing context classloader\\n- `safeLoaderSwapper()`: Returns a safe variant of LoaderSwap\\n\\n## LoaderSwap - Context Switching\\n\\n**LoaderSwap** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java): Implements AutoCloseable for automatic classloader restoration:\\n```java\\ntry (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = plugins.withClassLoader(pluginClassLoader)) {\\n    plugin.configure(config);\\n    // Operations here execute with pluginClassLoader as context\\n}\\n// Original classloader automatically restored\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration and Dependency Resolution\\n\\n**ConnectorConfig** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/ConnectorConfig.java): Base configuration class for connectors\\n- Defines standard connector configuration keys\\n- Includes key.converter and value.converter dependency injection\\n- Validates configuration and creates typed plugin instances\\n\\n**SourceConnectorConfig** and **SinkConnectorConfig**: Connector-specific configuration subclasses\\n\\n## REST API and Plugin Metadata\\n\\n**ConnectorPluginsResource** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorPluginsResource.java): REST endpoint providing:\\n- GET /connector-plugins: Lists all installed connector plugins\\n- GET /connector-plugins/{plugin-type}/config: Configuration schema for a plugin\\n\\n**PluginInfo** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489:connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/PluginInfo.java): DTO containing plugin metadata (className, type, version)\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Interface-Based Plugin Architecture**: All plugins implement standard interfaces (Connector, Converter, HeaderConverter, etc.)\\n\\n2. **Multi-Level Classloading with Child-First Delegation**: \\n   - PluginClassLoader loads plugin-specific classes\\n   - DelegatingClassLoader orchestrates multiple isolated plugin loaders\\n   - Prevents version conflicts between plugins\\n\\n3. **Reflection-Based Discovery**: Uses classgraph library to scan classpath for implementations\\n\\n4. **ServiceLoader Integration**: Modern Java SPI mechanism for declarative plugin discovery via META-INF/services\\n\\n5. **Dependency Injection via Context Switching**: LoaderSwap and withClassLoader enable the runtime to ensure plugins execute with the correct classloader context, allowing dependency injection through standard Java interfaces like Configurable\\n\\n6. **Version Management**: PluginDesc supports multi-versioning, allowing different versions of the same plugin to coexist\\n\\n7. **Lazy Instantiation**: Plugins are discovered at scan time but instantiated only when needed\\n\\nThis architecture enables Kafka Connect to load and manage plugins with complete isolation, preventing classpath conflicts while maintaining clean interface-based contracts for dependency injection.\"\n}\n",

PluginClassLoader loads plugin-specific classes\\n   - DelegatingClassLoader orchestrates multiple isolated plugin loaders\\n   - Prevents version conflicts between plugins\\n\\n3. **Reflection-Based Discovery**: Uses classgraph library to scan classpath for implementations\\n\\n4. **ServiceLoader Integration**: Modern Java SPI mechanism for declarative plugin discovery via META-INF/services\\n\\n5. **Dependency Injection via Context Switching**: LoaderSwap and withClassLoader enable the runtime to ensure plugins execute with the correct classloader context, allowing dependency injection through standard Java interfaces like Configurable\\n\\n6. **Version Management**: PluginDesc supports multi-versioning, allowing different versions of the same plugin to coexist\\n\\n7. **Lazy Instantiation**: Plugins are discovered at scan time but instantiated only when needed\\n\\nThis architecture enables Kafka Connect to load and manage plugins with complete isolation, preventing classpath conflicts while maintaining clean interface-based contracts for dependency injection.\"\n}\n",
